### Round 2: Brazilian Grand Prix
*Date: 1997-03-30*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 4: San Marino Grand Prix
*Date: 1997-04-27*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 6: Spanish Grand Prix
*Date: 1997-05-25*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 8: French Grand Prix
*Date: 1997-06-29*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 10: German Grand Prix
*Date: 1997-07-27*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 12: Belgian Grand Prix
*Date: 1997-08-24*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 14: Austrian Grand Prix
*Date: 1997-09-21*

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 16: Japanese Grand Prix
*Date: 1997-10-12*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
